[30;1m140 | [0m[35m    Checks if a string is formatted as "snake case".[0m
[30;1m141 | [0m[35m    A string is considered snake case when:[0m
[30;1m142 | [0m[35m    - it's composed only by lowercase/uppercase letters and digits[0m
[30;1m143 | [0m[35m    - it contains at least one underscore[0m
[30;1m144 | [0m[35m    - it does not start with a number[0m
[30;1m145 | [0m[35m    *Examples:*[0m
[30;1m146 | [0m[35m    >>> is_snake_case('foo_bar_baz') # returns true[0m
